<h2 class="kt-adv-heading81208_619231-6a wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading81208_619231-6a">Get to know Cooklyx Founder!</h2>



<p class="has-theme-palette-3-color has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-a14593afc8a096b60065bc97c126002b">Founder &amp; Editor‑in‑Chief of <strong>Cooklyx</strong>, Amy is an Atlanta‑based AI Scientist who became on a mission to simplify healthy eating for busy lives. With a background in <strong>AI systems and culinary wellness</strong>, Amy created Cooklyx to bridge the gap between tech‑level efficiency and real‑world kitchens. Her Cooklyx philosophy? <em>Prep Smart. Eat Fresh. Every Day</em>!  </p>

<h4 class="kt-adv-heading81208_818d36-1e wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading81208_818d36-1e">Follow US</h4>



<p class="has-text-align-center has-small-font-size">For real-life meal prep wins, fresh ideas, and behind-the-scenes from Amy’s AI-to-kitchen journey!</p>
